if test -f /usr/local/bin/xxd; then \
  mv -f /usr/local/bin/xxd /usr/local/bin/xxd.rm; \
  rm -f /usr/local/bin/xxd.rm; \
fi
cp xxd/xxd /usr/local/bin
strip /usr/local/bin/xxd
chmod 755 /usr/local/bin/xxd

installing /usr/local/share/man/man1/xxd.1
cp -r ../runtime/tools/* /usr/local/share/vim/vim90/tools
cvs=`find /usr/local/share/vim/vim90/tools \( -name CVS -o -name AAPDIR \) -print`; \
      if test -n "$cvs"; then \
	 rm -rf $cvs; \
      fi
chmod 644 /usr/local/share/vim/vim90/tools/*
perlpath=`./which.sh perl` && sed -e "s+/usr/bin/perl+$perlpath+" ../runtime/tools/efm_perl.pl >/usr/local/share/vim/vim90/tools/efm_perl.pl
awkpath=`./which.sh nawk` && sed -e "s+/usr/bin/nawk+$awkpath+" ../runtime/tools/mve.awk >/usr/local/share/vim/vim90/tools/mve.awk; if test -z "$awkpath"; then \
	awkpath=`./which.sh gawk` && sed -e "s+/usr/bin/nawk+$awkpath+" ../runtime/tools/mve.awk >/usr/local/share/vim/vim90/tools/mve.awk; if test -z "$awkpath"; then \
	awkpath=`./which.sh awk` && sed -e "s+/usr/bin/nawk+$awkpath+" ../runtime/tools/mve.awk >/usr/local/share/vim/vim90/tools/mve.awk; fi; fi
chmod 755 `grep -l "^#!" /usr/local/share/vim/vim90/tools/*`

chmod 755 /usr/local/share/vim/vim90/lang

if test -n "" -a -f po/Makefile; then \
   cd po; make prefix=/usr/local LOCALEDIR=/usr/local/share/vim/vim90/lang \
   INSTALL_DATA=cp FILEMOD=644 install; \
fi
if test -d ../runtime/lang; then \
   cp ../runtime/lang/README.txt ../runtime/lang/*.vim /usr/local/share/vim/vim90/lang; \
   chmod 644 /usr/local/share/vim/vim90/lang/README.txt /usr/local/share/vim/vim90/lang/*.vim; \
fi
if test -d ../runtime/keymap; then \
   cp ../runtime/keymap/README.txt ../runtime/keymap/*.vim /usr/local/share/vim/vim90/keymap; \
   chmod 644 /usr/local/share/vim/vim90/keymap/README.txt /usr/local/share/vim/vim90/keymap/*.vim; \
fi
if test -n ""; then \
	/bin/sh install-sh -c -d /usr/local/share/icons/hicolor/48x48/apps /usr/local/share/icons/locolor/32x32/apps \
	/usr/local/share/icons/locolor/16x16/apps /usr/local/share/applications; \
fi
if test -d /usr/local/share/icons/hicolor/48x48/apps -a -w /usr/local/share/icons/hicolor/48x48/apps \
	-a ! -f /usr/local/share/icons/hicolor/48x48/apps/gvim.png; then \
   cp ../runtime/vim48x48.png /usr/local/share/icons/hicolor/48x48/apps/gvim.png; \
   if test -z "" -a -x "" \
	   -a -w /usr/local/share/icons/hicolor \
	   -a -f /usr/local/share/icons/hicolor/index.theme; then \
	 -q /usr/local/share/icons/hicolor; \
   fi \
fi

#!/usr/bin/bash
# https://github.com/vim/vim/blob/master/src/INSTALL
pushd ~
BVT_INSTALLER=apt-get
sudo ${BVT_INSTALLER} update
sudo apt install -y make
sudo apt install -y clang
sudo apt install -y libtool-bin

git clone https://github.com/vim/vim.git
pushd ~/vim/src
make
make test
sudo make install
